Question: We have three blocks. Lets call them A, B and C. A medium black square is in block A. Block B is to the right of block A. It contains a small yellow circle and one big blue square. Below and to the right of the big blue square there is the small yellow circle. Finally, we have block C which is to the right of block B. It contains a small yellow square. The small yellow square is below and to the left of a big yellow square. The big yellow square is touching the right edge of this block. What is to the right of the circle? a small yellow square or a big yellow square which is touching the right edge of a block? 0: small yellow square 1: big yellow square which is touching the right edge of a block 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, let's analyze the information given about the blocks and their contents:

1. **Block A**: Contains a medium black square. No other information is provided about this block.

2. **Block B**:
- Is to the right of Block A.
- Contains a small yellow circle and a big blue square.
- The small yellow circle is below and to the right of the big blue square.

3. **Block C**:
- Is to the right of Block B.
- Contains a small yellow square and a big yellow square.
- The small yellow square is below and to the left of the big yellow square.
- The big yellow square is touching the right edge of Block C.

Now, let's determine what is to the right of the small yellow circle in Block B:

- The small yellow circle is in Block B. Since Block C is to the right of Block B, we need to consider the contents of Block C.
- In Block C, there is a small yellow square and a big yellow square.
- The big yellow square is touching the right edge of Block C, meaning it is positioned on the far right side of Block C.
- The small yellow square is below and to the left of the big yellow square, meaning it is positioned to the left of the big yellow square.

Given this arrangement, the big yellow square, which is touching the right edge of Block C, is to the right of the small yellow circle in Block B.

Therefore, the answer is that the big yellow square, which is touching the right edge of a block, is to the right of the small yellow circle.

Question: We have three blocks, A, B and C. There is a medium yellow square in block A. To the left of block A there is block B which contains a small blue square and one big black triangle. It has one medium black triangle, a small black triangle and a medium black circle. This block also has a small blue circle. Below the medium black triangle there is a big black square. The medium black triangle is to the right of the small black triangle. To the right of and near to the medium black circle there is the small black triangle. To the right of the black shape which is to the right of the medium black circle there is the big black square. What is to the right of the medium black circle? a medium black triangle or a medium yellow square? 0: medium black triangle 1: medium yellow square 2: both of them 3: none of them
To solve this problem, we need to carefully analyze the spatial relationships described in the text.

1. **Block A**: Contains a medium yellow square.

2. **Block B**:
- Contains a small blue square and a big black triangle.
- The small blue square is far from, below, and to the left of the big black triangle.

3. **Block C**:
- Contains a medium black triangle, a small black triangle, a medium black circle, and a small blue circle.
- Below the medium black triangle, there is a big black square.
- The medium black triangle is to the right of the small black triangle.
- To the right of and near to the medium black circle, there is the small black triangle.
- To the right of the black shape which is to the right of the medium black circle, there is the big black square.

Now, let's focus on the specific question: What is to the right of the medium black circle?

- According to fact2, "To the right of and near to the medium black circle there is the small black triangle."
- This means the small black triangle is directly to the right of the medium black circle.

The question asks whether a medium black triangle or a medium yellow square is to the right of the medium black circle.

- The medium black triangle is mentioned to be to the right of the small black triangle, not directly to the right of the medium black circle.
- The medium yellow square is in Block A, which is above Block C, and not directly related to the position of the medium black circle in Block C.

Therefore, neither the medium black triangle nor the medium yellow square is directly to the right of the medium black circle. The small black triangle is the shape directly to the right of the medium black circle.

To solve this problem, we need to analyze the spatial arrangement of the blocks and the squares within them.

1. **Block Arrangement:**
- From , Block A is to the right of Block C.
- From , Block C is to the right of Block B.
- Therefore, the order from left to right is: Block B, Block C, Block A.

2. **Squares in Block B:**
- From , Block B has one medium blue square.

3. **Squares in Block C:**
- From , Block C has a medium blue square.

4. **Squares in Block A:**
- Block A has two medium yellow squares and one medium black square.
- From the description, below the medium black square, there is medium yellow square number two.
- Below medium yellow square number two and the medium black square, there is medium yellow square number one.

5. **Position of Medium Yellow Squares:**
- Medium yellow square number one is at the bottom.
- Medium yellow square number two is above medium yellow square number one.
- The medium black square is above medium yellow square number one and at the same level as medium yellow square number two.

6. **Determining the Position Relative to Medium Blue Squares:**
- The medium blue squares are in Blocks B and C.
- Since Block A is to the right of Block C, all squares in Block A are to the right of the medium blue square in Block C.

- Block C contains two small black circles and one medium black square.

- The medium black square is below and to the right of small black circle number two.

- Block B contains a big yellow circle, a small blue circle, a medium blue triangle, and a small yellow square.
